PUBLIC NOTICES
Alf Insurance Services Private Limited
No. 115 &166 G.N. Chetty Road, T. Nagar, Chennai-600 017,
FTIMES NEW ROMAN
FORM No. 155
(See Rue 329)
Members Winding Up
Notice Convening Final Meeting
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 that a General Meeting of the Members of the above named
Company will be held on 25-02-2016 at No. 115 & 166 G.N. Chetty Road, T. Nagar, Chennai-600 017, at 10.00 AM for
the purpose of having an account laid before the members showing them the manner in which the winding up has been
conducted and the property of the company disposed of and of hearing any explanation that may be given by the liquidator
and also of determining by a special resolution of the company, the manner in which the books, accounts and documents
of the company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.
Chennai,
5th January 2016.

S. PRASAD,
Liquidator.

It is hereby notified that Ms.K. Manimekalai, daughter of Thiru Krishnan-Kamalam of Nagarcoil married Mr. Mohan,
son of Thiru. Ganesan - Valliammal of Nagarcoil on 20-04-1997 and that Mohan has suddenly expired on 15-09-2005 leaving
behind a son by name V.M. Velavan.
It is also notified that the above said Manimekalai remarried Mr. V. Vadivel son of Velusamy of Udumalpet on
23-02-2010 which has been registered. As I am now the Step-Father of Velavan, I want my son to bear the first letters of
both of us (Vadivel & Manimekalai). Therefore, I as the step-father of Velavan declare that his name shall remain the same
as V.M. Velavan.
Chennai,
8th January 2016.

V. VADIVEL,
(Step Father.)
